## 📊 PERFORMANCE BENCHMARKS & TARGETS

**The system MUST meet these specific performance targets:**

### Page Load Performance
- [ ] **Initial page load**: < 2 seconds (first contentful paint)
- [ ] **Time to interactive**: < 3 seconds
- [ ] **Full page load**: < 4 seconds
- [ ] **Dashboard load**: < 1.5 seconds (most critical page)
- [ ] **Time entries list (100 entries)**: < 2 seconds
- [ ] **Time entries list (1000 entries)**: < 3 seconds (with pagination)
- [ ] **Reports generation**: < 5 seconds (for monthly reports)
- [ ] **Export generation**: < 10 seconds (for large datasets)

### API Performance
- [ ] **Clock-in/out API**: < 200ms response time
- [ ] **Time entry CRUD**: < 300ms response time
- [ ] **Absence request**: < 400ms response time
- [ ] **Manager approval**: < 300ms response time
- [ ] **Compliance check**: < 500ms response time
- [ ] **Report generation API**: < 2 seconds (for daily reports)
- [ ] **Export API**: < 5 seconds (for monthly exports)

### Database Performance
- [ ] **Query execution**: < 100ms (95th percentile)
- [ ] **Complex queries**: < 500ms (95th percentile)
- [ ] **No N+1 query problems**: Verified with query profiler
- [ ] **All indexes created**: Verified with EXPLAIN queries
- [ ] **Database connection pool**: Properly configured
- [ ] **Query caching**: Enabled where appropriate

### Resource Usage
- [ ] **Memory usage**: < 128MB per request (average)
- [ ] **CPU usage**: < 50% per request (average)
- [ ] **Database connections**: < 10 concurrent connections (average)
- [ ] **File size limits**: CSS < 200KB, JS < 300KB (minified)

### Scalability Targets
- [ ] **Concurrent users**: Support 100+ concurrent users
- [ ] **Time entries**: Support 1,000,000+ time entries
- [ ] **Users**: Support 10,000+ users
- [ ] **Daily transactions**: Support 10,000+ clock-in/out operations per day

**Verification:** Use browser DevTools (Network tab, Performance tab), database query profiler, and load testing tools to verify all benchmarks are met.

8. **Mobile Scenario**: Employee uses app on mobile device
9. **Offline Scenario**: Employee works offline, syncs later
10. **Error Recovery Scenario**: System recovers from database error

## 🔄 DATA MIGRATION STRATEGY

**If migrating from existing system or Vue.js version:**

### Pre-Migration
- [ ] **Data backup**: Complete backup of all data before migration
- [ ] **Migration plan**: Detailed step-by-step migration plan
- [ ] **Migration script**: Automated migration script created
- [ ] **Test migration**: Test migration on copy of production data
- [ ] **Validation**: Verify migrated data is correct
- [ ] **Rollback plan**: Plan to rollback if migration fails
- [ ] **Downtime window**: Schedule migration during low-usage period

### Migration Steps
1. [ ] **Backup database**: Full database backup
2. [ ] **Backup files**: Backup any file uploads
3. [ ] **Run migration script**: Execute migration
4. [ ] **Validate data**: Check data integrity
5. [ ] **Test functionality**: Verify all features work
6. [ ] **Monitor errors**: Watch for errors in logs
7. [ ] **User verification**: Have users verify their data

### Post-Migration
- [ ] **Data verification**: All data migrated correctly
- [ ] **Functionality verification**: All features work
- [ ] **Performance verification**: Performance is acceptable
- [ ] **User communication**: Inform users of migration completion
- [ ] **Monitor for issues**: Watch for issues for 48 hours
- [ ] **Keep backup**: Keep backup for 30 days

### Rollback Procedure
- [ ] **Rollback script**: Automated rollback script ready
- [ ] **Rollback tested**: Tested on copy of production data
- [ ] **Rollback time**: Can rollback within 1 hour
- [ ] **Data preservation**: No data loss during rollback

## 🚀 DEPLOYMENT RUNBOOK

**Step-by-step deployment procedure:**

### Pre-Deployment Checklist
- [ ] All phases complete (0-30)
- [ ] All tests pass
- [ ] All quality gates passed
- [ ] Code review complete
- [ ] Security audit complete
- [ ] Performance audit complete
- [ ] Documentation complete
- [ ] Backup created
- [ ] Rollback plan ready
- [ ] Deployment window scheduled
- [ ] Team notified

### Deployment Steps
1. [ ] **Create deployment branch**: Tag release version
2. [ ] **Run pre-deployment tests**: All tests pass
3. [ ] **Backup production**: Full backup
4. [ ] **Deploy code**: Deploy new code
5. [ ] **Run database migrations**: Execute migrations
6. [ ] **Clear caches**: Clear all caches
7. [ ] **Verify deployment**: Check version, check logs
8. [ ] **Smoke tests**: Quick functionality tests
9. [ ] **Monitor errors**: Watch error logs
10. [ ] **User communication**: Inform users of deployment

### Post-Deployment Verification
- [ ] **Functionality**: All features work
- [ ] **Performance**: Performance is acceptable
- [ ] **Errors**: No critical errors in logs
- [ ] **User feedback**: Collect initial user feedback
- [ ] **Monitor**: Monitor for 24-48 hours
- [ ] **Documentation**: Update deployment log

### Rollback Procedure (if needed)
1. [ ] **Identify issue**: Document the problem
2. [ ] **Decision**: Decide to rollback
3. [ ] **Notify team**: Inform team of rollback
4. [ ] **Execute rollback**: Run rollback script
5. [ ] **Verify rollback**: Confirm system is back to previous state
6. [ ] **Investigate issue**: Root cause analysis
7. [ ] **Fix issue**: Fix the problem
8. [ ] **Re-deploy**: Deploy again after fix

## 📈 MONITORING & ALERTING

**Production monitoring requirements:**

### Metrics to Monitor
- [ ] **Page load times**: Track average and 95th percentile
- [ ] **API response times**: Track all API endpoints
- [ ] **Database query times**: Track slow queries
- [ ] **Error rates**: Track error frequency
- [ ] **User activity**: Track active users, clock-ins, etc.
- [ ] **System resources**: CPU, memory, disk usage
- [ ] **Database size**: Track database growth
- [ ] **Compliance violations**: Track violation frequency

### Alerts to Configure
- [ ] **High error rate**: Alert if error rate > 1%
- [ ] **Slow performance**: Alert if response time > 5 seconds
- [ ] **Database issues**: Alert on database errors
- [ ] **High resource usage**: Alert if CPU/memory > 80%
- [ ] **Disk space**: Alert if disk space < 20%
- [ ] **Failed logins**: Alert on suspicious login attempts
- [ ] **Compliance violations**: Alert on critical violations

### Logging Requirements
- [ ] **All errors logged**: With stack traces
- [ ] **All security events logged**: Login, logout, permission changes
- [ ] **All compliance violations logged**: With details
- [ ] **All data changes logged**: Audit trail
- [ ] **Performance metrics logged**: Response times, query times
- [ ] **Log retention**: Keep logs for 90 days minimum
- [ ] **Log rotation**: Prevent log files from growing too large

## 🔍 CODE REVIEW CHECKLIST

**Before merging any code, verify:**

### Code Quality
- [ ] Code follows PSR standards
- [ ] Code follows projectcheck patterns
- [ ] Code uses proper naming conventions
- [ ] Code is well-documented (PHPDoc, JSDoc)
- [ ] Code has no TODOs, FIXMEs, placeholders
- [ ] Code has no hardcoded values
- [ ] Code has no console.log statements
- [ ] Code has no commented-out code (unless necessary)

### Functionality
- [ ] Feature works as intended
- [ ] Feature handles errors gracefully
- [ ] Feature has proper validation
- [ ] Feature has proper permission checks
- [ ] Feature works with real data (no mocks)

### Security
- [ ] **Security architecture implemented** (defense in depth, least privilege, fail-secure)
- [ ] **Input validation implemented** (server-side, type, length, format, business rules)
- [ ] **Output escaping implemented** (XSS prevention, context-aware escaping)
- [ ] **SQL injection prevented** (parameterized queries everywhere)
- [ ] **XSS prevented** (all output escaped, CSP headers)
- [ ] **CSRF protection implemented** (tokens on all forms, validated server-side)
- [ ] **Role & permission model verified** (all test cases pass, penetration testing complete)
- [ ] **Permission checks implemented** (controller, service, template, database layers)
- [ ] **Data filtering by role** (employees see own, managers see team, admins see all)
- [ ] **Edge cases handled securely** (user deletion, role changes, concurrent access)
- [ ] **No information leakage** (generic error messages, no data hints)
- [ ] **Audit logging** (all security-relevant actions logged)
- [ ] **Security headers configured** (CSP, X-Frame-Options, X-Content-Type-Options, etc.)
- [ ] **Nextcloud best practices followed** (architecture, patterns, conventions)
- [ ] **No secrets in code** (use Nextcloud config system)

### Performance
- [ ] No N+1 query problems
- [ ] Database queries optimized
- [ ] Proper indexes used
- [ ] Caching used where appropriate
- [ ] No unnecessary database calls

### Testing
- [ ] Unit tests written (if applicable)
- [ ] Tests pass
- [ ] Edge cases considered
- [ ] Manual testing done

### Compliance
- [ ] ArbZG compliance maintained
- [ ] GDPR compliance maintained
- [ ] CSP/CORS compliance maintained
- [ ] Accessibility maintained
